Question #122 (ID: 415463)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}+y^{2}=36................(i)[/math] [math]f(y)=y-1, g(y)=y^{2}+4......(ii)[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int \frac{1}{1+\cos 4 x} d x[/math] = নির্ণয় কর
খ. [math](i)[/math] এ বর্ণিত বৃত্তের [math]x[/math] অক্ষের উপরের অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল সমাকলন পদ্ধতিতে নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\int \frac{f(y)+1}{f(y) g(y)} d y[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\int \frac{1}{1+\cos 4 x} d x=\int \frac{1}{2 \cos ^{2} 2 x} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \int \sec ^{2} 2 x d x=\frac{1}{2} \frac{\tan 2 x}{2}+c=\frac{1}{4} \tan 2 x+c\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় যোজিত ফল [math]\frac{1}{4} \tan 2 x+c[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=36......[/math]
(i)[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow y^{2}=36-x^{2}\\\Rightarrow y=\sqrt{36-x^{2}}\end{array}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\begin{array}{l}x=6 \sin \theta \\d x=6 \cos \theta d \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline x & 0 & 6 \\\hline \theta & 0 & \frac{\pi}{2} \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=2 \int_{0}^{6} y \cdot d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \int_{0}^{6} \sqrt{36-x^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sqrt{36-36 \sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot 6 \cos \theta d \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 6 \cdot 6 \sqrt{1-\sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot \cos \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow 72 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \cos ^{2} \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow 36 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}(1+\cos 2 \theta) d \theta \\\Rightarrow 36\left[\theta+\frac{\sin 2 \theta}{2}\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}=36[\theta+\sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 36\left[\left(\frac{\pi}{2}+0\right)-(0+0)\right]=18 \pi[/math]
 বর্গ এককনির্ণেয় x-অক্ষের উপরের অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]18 \pi[/math]
 বর্গ একক ।গদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(\mathrm{y})=\mathrm{y}-1[/math]
এবং [math]g(y)=y^{2}+4[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\int \frac{f(y)+1}{f(y) g(y)} d y=\int \frac{y-1+1}{(y-1)\left(y^{2}+4\right)} d y[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int \frac{y}{(y-1)\left(y^{2}+4\right)} d y=\int \frac{(y-1)+1}{(y-1)\left(y^{2}+4\right)} d y \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{1}{y^{2}+4} d y+\int \frac{1}{(y-1)\left(y^{2}+4\right)} d y \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \int\left\{\frac{1}{y-1}-\frac{y+1}{y^{2}+4}\right\} d y \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \ln |y-1|-\frac{1}{5} \int\left(\frac{y}{y^{2}+4}+\frac{1}{y^{2}+4}\right) d y \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \ln |y-1|-\frac{1}{2.5} \ln \left|y^{2}+4\right|-\frac{1}{5.2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \ln |y-1|-\frac{1}{10} \ln \left|y^{2}+4\right|-\frac{1}{10} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+c \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{1}{2}-\frac{1}{10}\right) \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \ln |y-1|-\frac{1}{10} \ln \left|y^{2}+4\right|+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{5} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \ln |y-1|-\frac{1}{10} \ln \left|y^{2}+4\right|+c\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় যোজিত ফল [math]\frac{2}{5} \tan ^{-1} \frac{y}{2}+\frac{1}{5} \ln |y-1|-\frac{1}{10} \ln \left|y^{2}+4\right|+c[/math]


Explanation:
ক কারণ [math]1+\cos 4x=2\cos^{2}2x[/math], তাই অন্তরকটি [math]\frac{1}{1+\cos4x}=\frac{1}{2\cos^{2}2x}=\tfrac{1}{2}\sec^{2}2x[/math] হয় এবং [math]\int \tfrac{1}{2}\sec^{2}2x\,dx=\tfrac{1}{2}\cdot\tfrac{1}{2}\tan2x+C=\tfrac{1}{4}\tan2x+C[/math].

খ বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ [math]6[/math] হওয়ায় উপরের অর্ধবৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল হল অর্ধেক মূল ক্ষেত্রফল: [math]\tfrac{1}{2}\pi r^{2}=\tfrac{1}{2}\pi\cdot6^{2}=18\pi[/math]; সমাকলনভাবে [math]\int_{-6}^{6}\sqrt{36-x^{2}}\,dx=18\pi[/math] (উদাহরণস্বরূপ [math]x=6\sin t[/math] বদলে নেওয়া যায়)।

গ প্রথমে [math]f(y)=y-1\Rightarrow f(y)+1=y[/math], তাই অন্তরক হচ্ছে [math]\int\frac{y}{(y-1)(y^{2}+4)}dy[/math]; ভাঙলে [math]\frac{y}{(y-1)(y^{2}+4)}=\frac{1/5}{y-1}-\frac{1/5\,y}{y^{2}+4}+\frac{4/5}{y^{2}+4}[/math] হয় এবং সমাকলন করলে ফল পাওয়া যায়: [math]\frac{1}{5}\ln|y-1|-\frac{1}{10}\ln(y^{2}+4)+\frac{2}{5}\arctan\frac{y}{2}+C[/math].

Question #123 (ID: 415461)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\cos x, g(x, y)=9 x^{2}+25 y^{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. সমাকলন কর [math]\int \frac{d x}{4 f\left(\cos ^{-1} x^{2}\right)+9}[/math]
খ. [math]\int_{1}^{3} \frac{1}{x} \sqrt{1-\{f(\ln x)\}^{2}} dx[/math] - এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]g(x, y)=225[/math] উপবৃত্ত দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\cos x[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\int \frac{d x}{4 f\left(\cos ^{-1} x^{2}\right)+9}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int \frac{d x}{4 \cos \left(\cos ^{-1} x^{2}\right)+9} \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{d x}{4 x^{2}+9}=\int \frac{1}{4\left(x^{2}+\frac{9}{4}\right)} d x=\frac{1}{4} \int \frac{1}{x^{2}+\left(\frac{3}{2}\right)^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{1}{\frac{3}{2}} \tan ^{-1} \frac{2 x}{3}+c=\frac{2}{12} \tan ^{-1} \frac{2 x}{3}+c=\frac{1}{6} \tan ^{-1} \frac{2 x}{3}+c\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় সমাকলিত ফল [math]\frac{1}{6} \tan ^{-1} \frac{2 x}{3}+c .[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\cos x[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\int_{1}^{3} \frac{1}{x} \sqrt{1-\{f(\ln x)\}^{2}} \mathrm{dx}[/math]
ধরি, [math]\ln x=y[/math]
 [math]\frac{1}{x} d x=d y[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline x & 1 & 3 \\\hline y & 0 & \ln 3 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int_{1}^{3} \frac{1}{x} \sqrt{1-\{\cos (\ln x)\}^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\ln 3} \sqrt{1-(\cos y)^{2}} d y \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\ln 3} \sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} y} d y \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\ln 3} \sqrt{\sin ^{2} y} d y \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\ln 3} \sin y d y=[-\cos y]_{0}^{\ln 3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -[\cos (\ln 3)-\cos 0] \\\Rightarrow -\cos (\ln 3)+1=1-\cos (\ln 3)\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]1-\cos (\ln 3) .[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]{g}(x, y)=9 x^{2}+25 y^{2}[/math]
আবার, [math]g(x, y)=225[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 9 x^{2}+25 y^{2}=225\\\Rightarrow 25 y^{2}=225-9 x^{2}\\\Rightarrow 25 y^{2}=9\left(25-x^{2}\right)\\\Rightarrow y^{2}=\frac{9}{25}\left(25-x^{2}\right)\\\Rightarrow y=\frac{3}{5} \sqrt{25-x^{2}}\end{array}[/math]

[Image]
উপবৃত্তটি দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 \int_{0}^{5} y d x \\\Rightarrow 4 \int_{0}^{5} \frac{3}{5} \sqrt{25-x^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{12}{5} \int_{0}^{5} \sqrt{25-x^{2}} d x\end{array}[/math]
ধরি, [math]x=5 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{dx}=5 \cos \theta d \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline x & 0 & 5 \\\hline \theta & 0 & \frac{\pi}{2} \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{12}{5} \int^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sqrt{25-25 \sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot 5 \cos \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow 12\left[5 \sqrt{1-\sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot \cos \theta d \theta\right. \\\Rightarrow 60\left[\cos ^{2} \theta d \theta\right. \\\Rightarrow 30\{(1+\cos 2 \theta) d \theta \\\Rightarrow 30\left[\theta+\frac{\sin 2 \theta}{2}\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \\\Rightarrow 30\left[\left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{\sin \pi}{2}\right)-(0+0)\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=15 \pi[/math]
 বর্গ এককনির্ণেয় উপবৃত্ত দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=15 \pi[/math]
 বর্গ একক ।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক যেহেতু [math]f(\cos^{-1}x^{2})=\cos(\cos^{-1}x^{2})=x^{2}[/math] (এখানে ধরে নেবো [math]|x|\le1[/math]), অন্তরকটি হয় [math]\int\frac{dx}{4x^{2}+9}[/math] এবং এটি সমাধান করে [math]\frac{1}{6}\tan^{-1}\frac{2x}{3}+C[/math]।
খ [math]f(\ln x)=\cos(\ln x)[/math], তাই [math]\sqrt{1-\cos^{2}(\ln x)}=|\sin(\ln x)|[/math]; কিন্তু [math]\ln x\in[0,\ln3]গ উপবৃত্তটি হল [math]9x^{2}+25y^{2}=225\iff\frac{x^{2}}{25}+\frac{y^{2}}{9}=1[/math], তাই অর্ধদৈর্ঘ্যগুলো [math]a=5,\,b=3[/math] এবং ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\pi ab=15\pi[/math]।

Question #124 (ID: 415462)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\frac{1}{x^{2}(x-1)^{\prime}}[/math]

একটি পরাবৃত্তের সমীকরণ, [math]y^{2}=6 x[/math]

ও একটি সরলরেখার সমীকরণ [math]y=x[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int x \ln x^{2} d x[/math] [math]\int x \ln x^{2} d x =[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int f(x) d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. উদ্দীপকের পরাবৃত্ত ও সরলরেখা দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{aligned}& \int x \ln x^{2} d x \\\Rightarrow & \ln x^{2} \int x d x-\int\left\{\frac{d}{d x} \ln x^{2} \int x d x\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow & \frac{x^{2}}{2} \ln x^{2}-\int \frac{1}{x^{2}} \cdot 2 x \cdot \frac{x^{2}}{2} d x=\frac{x^{2}}{2} \ln x^{2}-\int x d x \\\Rightarrow & \frac{x^{2}}{2} \ln x^{2}-\frac{x^{2}}{2}+c=\frac{x^{2}}{2}\left(\ln x^{2}-1\right)+c\end{aligned}[/math]
নির্ণেয় যোজিত ফল [math]\frac{x^{2}}{2}\left(\ln x^{2}-1\right)+c .[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\frac{1}{x^{2}(x-1)}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\int f(x) \mathrm{dx}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int \frac{1}{x^{2}(x-1)} d x=\int \frac{1}{x}\left\{\frac{1}{x(x-1)}\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{1}{x}\left\{\frac{1}{(x-1)}+\frac{1}{x(-1)}\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{1}{x}\left\{\frac{1}{x-1}-\frac{1}{x}\right\} d x=\int \frac{1}{x(x-1)} d x-\int \frac{1}{x^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \int\left(\frac{1}{x-1}-\frac{1}{x}\right) d x-\int x^{-2} d x \\\Rightarrow \ln |x-1|-\ln |x|-\frac{x^{-2+1}}{-2+1}+c \\\Rightarrow \ln |x-1|-\ln |x|+\frac{1}{x}+c\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় যোজিত ফল [math]\ln |x-1|-\ln |x|+\frac{1}{x}+c[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]y^{2}=6 x......[/math]
(1)এবং [math]y=x.......[/math]
(2)(1) নং এ y = x বসিয়ে[math]\begin{array}{l}x^{2}=6 x\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{x}^{2}-6 \mathrm{x}=0\\\Rightarrow x(x-6)=0\\\therefore x=0, x=6\end{array}[/math]
এখানে, [math]y_{1}^{2}=6 x[/math]
 এবং [math]y_{2}=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow y_{1}= \pm \sqrt{6 x}[/math]
 এবং x-অক্ষেরউপরে [math]\mathrm{y}_{1}[/math]
 ধনাত্মক ।আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\int_{0}^{6}\left(y_{1}-y_{2}\right) d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{6}(\sqrt{6} x-x) d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{6}(\sqrt{6} \cdot \sqrt{x}-x) d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{6}\left(\sqrt{6} \cdot x^{\frac{1}{2}}-x\right) d x \\\Rightarrow \left[\sqrt{6} \cdot \frac{x^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{x^{2}}{2}\right]_{0}^{6} \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{2 \sqrt{6}}{3} \cdot 6^{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{36}{2}\right)-0 \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sqrt{6}}{3} \cdot 6 \sqrt{6}-18\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 24-18=6[/math]
 বর্গ এককনির্ণেয় আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]6[/math]
 বর্গ একক

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\int x\ln x^{2}\,dx[/math]: কারণ [math]\ln x^{2}=2\ln|x|[/math], integrand = [math]2x\ln|x|[/math]. অংশগত সমাকলনে [math]u=\ln|x|,\ dv=2x\,dx[/math] দিলে ফল পাওয়া যায় [math]x^{2}\ln|x|-\tfrac{x^{2}}{2}+C[/math]।

খ [math]\int f(x)\,dx[/math]: এখানে ধরে নিলাম [math]f(x)=\dfrac{1}{x^{2}(x-1)}[/math] এবং পার্শ্বভাগে বিভাজন করে [math]\dfrac{1}{x^{2}(x-1)}=\dfrac{-1}{x}+\dfrac{-1}{x^{2}}+\dfrac{1}{x-1}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, ফলে সমাকলন হচ্ছে [math]\int f(x)\,dx=-\ln|x|+\dfrac{1}{x}+\ln|x-1|+C=\ln\Big|\dfrac{x-1}{x}\Big|+\dfrac{1}{x}+C[/math]।

গ পরাবৃত্ত [math]y^{2}=6x\Rightarrow x=\dfrac{y^{2}}{6}[/math] এবং সরলরেখা [math]y=x\Rightarrow x=y[/math] মিলানোর সময় [math]y(y-6)=0[/math] থেকে [math]y=0,6[/math]. ক্ষেত্রফল (ডান−বাম) = [math]\int_{0}^{6}\Big(y-\dfrac{y^{2}}{6}\Big)dy=[\tfrac{y^{2}}{2}-\tfrac{y^{3}}{18}]_{0}^{6}=6[/math]।

Question #125 (ID: 415460)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P(x)=4 x+3, Q(x)=x[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\lim _{x \rightarrow 0} \frac{1-\cos x}{x}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int \frac{d x}{(2 x+1) \sqrt{p(x)}}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. ক্যালকুলাসের সাহায্যে [math]4\{Q(x)\}^{2}+9\{Q(y)\}^{2}=36[/math] বক্ররেখাটি দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\lim _{x \rightarrow 0} \frac{1-\cos x}{x}=\lim _{x \rightarrow 0} \frac{2 \sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{x}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{x}{2} \rightarrow 0 \frac{\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\frac{x}{2}} \cdot \frac{\lim }{\frac{x}{2} \rightarrow 0} \frac{\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\frac{x}{2}} \lim _{x \rightarrow 0} \frac{x}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1 \cdot 1 \cdot \frac{0}{2}=0 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]P(x)=4 x+3[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int \frac{d x}{(2 x+1) \sqrt{P(x)}}=\int \frac{d x}{(2 x+1) \sqrt{4 x+3}}[/math]
ধরি, [math]4 x+3=z^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 \mathrm{dx}=2 \mathrm{zdz}\\\therefore \mathrm{dx}=\frac{1}{2} \mathrm{zdz}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int \frac{\frac{1}{2} z d z}{\left\{2 \cdot \frac{z^{2}-3}{4}+1\right\} \cdot z}=\frac{1}{2} \int \frac{\mathrm{dz}}{\frac{z^{2}-3+2}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{\mathrm{dz}}{\mathrm{z}^{2}-1}=\frac{1}{2 \cdot 1} \ln \left|\frac{\mathrm{z}-1}{\mathrm{z}+1}\right|+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \ln \left|\frac{\sqrt{4 x+3}-1}{\sqrt{4 x+3}+1}\right|+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]Q(x)=x[/math]
এবং [math]4\{\mathrm{Q}(\mathrm{x})\}^{2}+9\{\mathrm{Q}(\mathrm{y})\}^{2}=36[/math]
 [math]\therefore 4 x^{2}+9 y^{2}=36 \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 9 y^{2}=36-4 x^{2} \\\Rightarrow 9 y^{2}=4\left(9-x^{2}\right) \\\Rightarrow y^{2}=\frac{4}{9}\left(9-x^{2}\right) \\\therefore y= \pm \frac{2}{3} \sqrt{9-x^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
প্রথম চতুর্ভাগে উপবৃত্তটির জন্য [math]y=\frac{2}{3} \sqrt{9-x^{2}}[/math]
(i) নং এ y = 0 বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}4 x^{2}=36 \Rightarrow x^{2}=9 \\\therefore x= \pm 3\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ উপবৃত্তটি x-অক্ষকে [math](3, 0)[/math]
 ও [math](-3, 0)[/math]
 বিন্দুতে ছেদ করে ।[math]\therefore[/math]
 উপবৃত্তটি দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 \times \int_{0}^{3} \frac{2}{3} \sqrt{9-x^{2}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow \frac{8}{3} \int_{0}^{3} \sqrt{3^{2}-x^{2}} \mathrm{dx}\end{array}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{8}{3}\left[\frac{x \sqrt{3^{2}-x^{2}}}{2}+\frac{3^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1}\left(\frac{x}{3}\right)\right]_{0}^{3} \\\Rightarrow \frac{8}{3}\left[0+\frac{9}{2} \sin ^{-1}(1)-0-0\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{8}{3} \times \frac{9}{2} \times \frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 6 \pi[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\lim_{x\to0}\frac{1-\cos x}{x}[/math] এ [math]\cos x\approx1-\tfrac{x^2}{2}[/math] বলা যায়, ফলে ভগ্নাংশের অগ্রগামিতার প্রধান ধাপ [math]\frac{x^2/2}{x}=\tfrac{x}{2}\to0[/math]; তাই সীমা শূন্য।

খ যদি [math]p(x)=P(x)=4x+3[/math] ধরা হয়, তবে [math]u=\sqrt{4x+3}[/math] নেয়া হলে [math]dx=\tfrac{u}{2}\,du[/math] এবং [math]2x+1=\tfrac{u^2-1}{2}[/math] হয়ে ইন্টিগ্রালটি [math]\int\frac{du}{u^2-1}=\tfrac{1}{2}\ln\left|\frac{u-1}{u+1}\right|+C[/math] হয়, ফলে ফলাফল [math]\tfrac{1}{2}\ln\left|\frac{\sqrt{4x+3}-1}{\sqrt{4x+3}+1}\right|+C[/math]।

গ [math]4x^2+9y^2=36[/math] কে ভাগ করলে [math]\frac{x^2}{9}+\frac{y^2}{4}=1[/math] পাওয়া যায়, যা অক্ষঅনুভূকী উপবৃত্ত; অয়ত্বারকরা [math]a=3,\;b=2[/math], ফলে ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\pi ab=6\pi[/math]।

Question #126 (ID: 415458)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প: [math]f(x)=x^{2} \sqrt{16-x^{2}}, g(x)=y^{2}-8 x[/math] এবং [math]h(x)=x^{2}-8 y[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int x \ln 2 x d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\int_{-2}^{2} f(x) d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. [math]g(x)=0[/math] এবং [math]h(x)=0[/math].বক্ররেখা দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\int x \ln 2 x d x \\\Rightarrow \ln 2 x \int x d x-\int\left\{\frac{d}{d x} \ln (2 x) \int x d x\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow \ln 2 x \cdot \frac{x^{2}}{2}-\int\left\{\frac{1}{2 x} \cdot 2 \cdot \frac{x^{2}}{2}\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2} \ln 2 x}{2}-\int \frac{x}{2} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2} \ln 2 x}{2}-\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{x^{2}}{2}+c=\frac{x^{2} \ln 2 x}{2}-\frac{x^{2}}{4}+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x^{2} \sqrt{16-x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int_{-2}^{2} f(x) d x=\int_{-2}^{2} x^{2} \sqrt{16-x^{2}} d x[/math]
ধরি, [math]x=4 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{dx}=4 \cos \theta \mathrm{d} \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline x & -2 & 2 \\\hline \theta & -\frac{\pi}{6} & \frac{\pi}{6} \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \mathrm{I} & =\int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}} 16 \sin ^{2} \theta \sqrt{16-16 \sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot 4 \cos \theta d \theta \\&\Rightarrow \int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}} 16 \sin ^{2} \theta \cdot 4 \sqrt{1-\sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot 4 \cos \theta d \theta \\& \Rightarrow \int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}} 256 \sin ^{2} \theta \cdot \cos ^{2} \theta d \theta \\& \Rightarrow 64 \int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}}(2 \sin \theta \cos \theta)^{2} d \theta \\& \Rightarrow 64 \int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}}(\sin 2 \theta)^{2} d \theta\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 32 \int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}} 2 \sin ^{2} 2 \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow 32 \int_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}}(1-\cos 4 \theta) d \theta \\\Rightarrow 32\left[\theta-\frac{\sin 4 \theta}{4}\right]_{-\frac{\pi}{6}}^{\frac{\pi}{6}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 32\left[\frac{\pi}{6}-\frac{1}{4} \cdot \sin \frac{2 \pi}{3}+\frac{\pi}{6}+\frac{1}{4} \sin \left(\frac{-2 \pi}{3}\right)\right] \\\Rightarrow 32\left[\frac{\pi}{3}-\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right] \\\Rightarrow 32\left[\frac{\pi}{3}-\frac{2 \sqrt{3}}{8}\right]=\frac{32 \pi}{3}-8 \sqrt{3} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]g(x)=y^{2}-8 x[/math]
এবং [math]h(x)=x^{2}-8 y[/math]
আবার, [math]g(x)=0[/math]
 এবং [math]h(x)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore y^{2}-8 x=0[/math]
অর্থাৎ, [math]y^{2}=8 \mathrm{x} \quad \therefore \mathrm{y}=2 \sqrt{2} \sqrt{\mathrm{x}}[/math]
এবং [math]x^{2}-8 y=0[/math]
 অর্থাৎ [math]x^{2}=8 y \quad \therefore y=\frac{x^{2}}{8}[/math]
মনে করি, [math]y_{1}=2 \sqrt{2} \sqrt{x}[/math]
 এবং [math]y_{2}=\frac{x^{2}}{8}[/math]
এখন, [math]2 \sqrt{2} \sqrt{x}=\frac{x^{2}}{8}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 8 x=\frac{x^{4}}{64} \\\Rightarrow 512 x=x^{4} \\\Rightarrow \left(x^{3}-512\right) x=0 \\\therefore x=0,8\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{x}=0[/math]
 হলে [math]y=0[/math]
 [math]x=8[/math]
 হলে [math]y=8[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 পরাবৃত্তদ্বয়ের ছেদবিন্দু [math]O(0, 0)[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{A}(8,8)[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\mathrm{OPAQO}[/math]
 ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{8}\left(y_{1}-y_{2}\right) d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{8}\left(2 \sqrt{2} \sqrt{x}-\frac{x^{2}}{8}\right) d x \\\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{2} \int_{0}^{8} \sqrt{x} d x-\frac{1}{8} \int_{0}^{8} x^{2} d x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{2}\left[\frac{x^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\frac{3}{2}}\right]_{0}^{8}-\frac{1}{8}\left[\frac{x^{3}}{3}\right]_{0}^{8}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{4 \sqrt{2}}{3}\left(8^{\frac{3}{2}}-0\right)-\frac{1}{24}\left(8^{3}-0\right) \\\Rightarrow \frac{4 \sqrt{2}}{3} \times 16 \sqrt{2}-\frac{64}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{128}{3}-\frac{64}{3}=\frac{64}{3}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক ইন্টিগ্রেশন বাই পার্টস নিলে [math]u=\ln(2x),\;dv=x\,dx[/math] পাই এবং ফল হচ্ছে [math]\int x\ln(2x)\,dx=\frac{x^{2}}{2}\ln(2x)-\frac{x^{2}}{4}+C[/math] (ডোমেইন মনে রাখবেন [math]x>0[/math])।

খ [math]f(x)=x^{2}\sqrt{16-x^{2}}[/math] হলো একক, তাই [math]\int_{-2}^{2}f(x)\,dx=2\int_{0}^{2}x^{2}\sqrt{16-x^{2}}\,dx[/math] এবং বদল [math]x=4\sin t[/math] ব্যবহার করলে উপসমীকরণ থেকে শেষ পর্যন্ত মান পাওয়া যায় [math]\frac{32\pi}{3}-8\sqrt{3}[/math]।

গ রেখাগুলো হলো [math]y^{2}=8x[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}=8y[/math], তাদের ছেদে [math]y=0[/math] ও [math]y=8[/math]; ক্ষেত্রফল হলো আনুভূমিক ইন্টিগ্রাল [math]\int_{0}^{8}\big(\sqrt{8y}-\frac{y^{2}}{8}\big)\,dy[/math] এবং সেটির মান [math]\frac{64}{3}[/math]।

Question #127 (ID: 415459)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board

Question:
[math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{d}{d x}\left\{\ln \sqrt{\frac{1-\cos x}{1+\cos x}}\right\}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\int \frac{d \theta}{1+3\left\{f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)\right\}^{2}}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\left\{1+f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)\right\}^{2} f(\mathrm{x}) \mathrm{dx}=\frac{7}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{d}{d x}\left\{\ln \sqrt{\left.\frac{1-\cos x}{1+\cos x}\right\}}\right\} \\\Rightarrow \frac{d}{d x}\left\{\ln \sqrt{\frac{2 \sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{2 \cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}}\right\}=\frac{d}{d x}\left(\ln \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}\right) \\\Rightarrow \frac{d}{d x}\left\{\ln \left(\tan \frac{x}{2}\right)\right\}=\frac{1}{\tan \frac{x}{2}} \frac{d}{d x}\left(\tan \frac{x}{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot \frac{x}{2} \cdot \sec ^{2} \frac{x}{2} \frac{d}{d x}\left(\frac{x}{2}\right)=\frac{\cos \frac{x}{2}}{\sin \frac{x}{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2 \sin \frac{x}{2} \cos \frac{x}{2}}=\frac{1}{\sin 2 \cdot \frac{x}{2}}=\frac{1}{\sin x}=\operatorname{cosecx} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]
ধরি, [math]I=\int \frac{d \theta}{1+3\left\{f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)\right\}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int \frac{d \theta}{1+3\left\{\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)\right\}^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{d \theta}{1+3 \cos ^{2} \theta}=\int \frac{d \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta\left(\frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \theta}+3\right)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\int \frac{\sec ^{2} \theta d \theta}{\sec ^{2} \theta+3}=\int \frac{\sec ^{2} \theta d \theta}{\tan ^{2} \theta+1+3}[/math]
ধরি,[math]\tan \theta=z[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec ^{2} \theta \mathrm{d} \theta=\mathrm{dz}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int \frac{\sec ^{2} \theta \mathrm{d} \theta}{\tan ^{2} \theta+2^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{\mathrm{dz}}{\mathrm{z}^{2}+2^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1}\left(\frac{\mathrm{z}}{2}\right)+\mathrm{c} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1}\left(\frac{\tan \theta}{2}\right)+\mathrm{c} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গবামপক্ষ [math]=\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\left\{1+f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)\right\}^{2} f(x) d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\left\{1+\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)\right\}^{2} \sin x d x[/math]
ধরি,[math]1+\cos x=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -\sin \mathrm{xdx}=\mathrm{dz} \\\therefore \sin \mathrm{xdx}=-\mathrm{dz}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline \mathrm{x} & \frac{\pi}{2} & 0 \\\hline \mathrm{z} & 1 & 2 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}(1+\cos x)^{2} \sin x d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{2}^{1} z^{2}(-d z) \\\Rightarrow \int_{1}^{2} z^{2} d z \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{z^{3}}{3}\right]_{1}^{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{3}\left(2^{3}-1^{3}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{3}(8-1)=\frac{7}{3}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\left\{1+f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{x}\right)\right\}^{2} f(\mathrm{x}) \mathrm{dx}=\frac{7}{3}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\frac{1-\cos x}{1+\cos x}=\tan^2\frac{x}{2}[/math] হওয়ায় অভিব্যক্তিটি হচ্ছে [math]\ln\big|\tan\frac{x}{2}\big|[/math]; তার আপেক্ষিক উৎপন্নক হলো [math]\frac{d}{dx}\ln\big|\tan\frac{x}{2}\big|=\frac{1}{2}\cdot\frac{\sec^2\frac{x}{2}}{\tan\frac{x}{2}}=\frac{1}{\sin x}[/math]।

খ এখানে [math]f\big(\tfrac{\pi}{2}-\theta\big)=\cos\theta[/math], তাই সমাকলন [math]\int\frac{d\theta}{1+3\cos^2\theta}=\int\frac{\sec^2\theta\,d\theta}{\tan^2\theta+4}[/math] হয়; [math]t=\tan\theta,\ dt=\sec^2\theta\,d\theta[/math] নিলে এটি [math]\int\frac{dt}{t^2+4}=\tfrac{1}{2}\arctan\frac{t}{2}+C=\tfrac{1}{2}\arctan\frac{\tan\theta}{2}+C[/math]।

গ কারণ [math]f\big(\tfrac{\pi}{2}-x\big)=\cos x[/math], ইনটিগ্র্যান্ড হচ্ছে [math](1+\cos x)^2\sin x[/math]; [math]u=1+\cos x,\ du=-\sin x\,dx[/math] এনে সীমা [math]u(0)=2,\ u(\tfrac{\pi}{2})=1[/math], ফলে ইন্টিগ্রাল [math]\int_0^{\pi/2}(1+\cos x)^2\sin x\,dx=\int_2^1 u^2(-du)=\int_1^2 u^2du=\frac{7}{3}[/math]।

Question #128 (ID: 415457)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board

Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প: [math]f(x)=\cos x, \cdot g(x)=2 x^{2}+2 y^{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int x e^{2 x^{2}} d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \frac{f(x)}{8+\{f(x)\}^{2}} d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. নির্দিষ্ট যোগজ ব্যবহার করে [math]g(x)=72[/math] বৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, [math]2 x^{2}=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 x d x=d z \\\therefore x d x=\frac{d z}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\int \mathrm{xe}^{2 \mathrm{x}^{2}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow\int \frac{1}{4} \cdot \mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{z}} \cdot \mathrm{dz} \\\Rightarrow\frac{1}{4} \mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{z}}+\mathrm{c} \\\Rightarrow\frac{1}{4} \mathrm{e}^{2 x^{2}}+\mathrm{c} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\cos x[/math]
ধরি, [math]z=\sin x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \mathrm{dz}=\cos \mathrm{x} \mathrm{dx}\\\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline \mathrm{x} & 0 & \frac{\pi}{2} \\\hline \mathrm{z} & 0 & 1 \\\hline\end{array}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \frac{\mathrm{f}(\mathrm{x})}{8+\{\mathrm{f}(\mathrm{x})\}^{2}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \frac{\cos \mathrm{x}}{8+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{x}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \frac{\cos \mathrm{x}}{9-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{x}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{1} \frac{\mathrm{dz}}{3^{2}-\mathrm{z}^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left[\frac{1}{2.3} \ln \left|\frac{3+z}{3-z}\right|\right]_{0}^{1} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{1}{6} \ln \left|\frac{3+z}{3-z}\right|\right]_{0}^{1} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{6}(\ln 2-\ln 1) \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{6} \ln 2 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]g(x)=2 x^{2}+2 y^{2}[/math]
এবং [math]g(x)=72[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}\Rightarrow 2 x^{2}+2 y^{2}=72 \\x^{2}+y^{2}=36 \\\Rightarrow y^{2}=36-x^{2} \\\therefore y= \pm \sqrt{6^{2}-x^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
x-অক্ষের উপরের অংশে y ধনাত্মকঅথাৎ [math]y=\sqrt{6^{2}-x^{2}}[/math]
নির্ণেয় ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=4 \int_{0}^{6} y d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 \int_{0}^{6} \sqrt{6^{2}-x^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow 4\left[\frac{x \sqrt{6^{2}-x^{2}}}{2}+\frac{6^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{6}\right]_{0}^{6} \\\Rightarrow 4\left(0+\frac{6^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} 1-0-0\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=4 \cdot \frac{36}{2}. \frac{\pi}{2}=36 \pi[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক সমীকরণে পরিবর্তনশীল প্রতিস্থাপন নিলে [math]u=2x^2,\ du=4x\,dx[/math] পাওয়া যায়, তাই [math]\int x e^{2x^2}dx=\frac{1}{4}e^{2x^2}+C[/math]।

খ substitution [math]u=\sin x,\ du=\cos x\,dx[/math] করলে সীমা [math]0\to0,\,\pi/2\to1[/math] এবং ইন্টিগ্রালটি হয় [math]\int_0^1\frac{du}{9-u^2}=\frac{1}{6}\ln\frac{3+u}{3-u}\Big|_0^1=\frac{1}{6}\ln 2[/math]।

গ সমীকরণকে দুই দিয়ে ভাগ করলে [math]x^2+y^2=36[/math] পাওয়া যায়, এর ব্যাসার্ধ [math]r=6[/math] তাই ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\pi r^2=36\pi[/math]।

Question #129 (ID: 415456)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board

Question:
[math]P_{1}(x)=x[/math] [math]P_{2}(x)=\cot ^{-1} x[/math]


[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\int_{2}^{5} \ln 2 x d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} P_{1}(x) P_{2}(x) d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. নির্দিষ্ট যোগজ ব্যবহার করে চিত্রের ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\int_{2}^{5} \ln 2 x d x \\\Rightarrow\left[\ln 2 x \int d x-\int\left\{\left(\frac{d}{d x} \ln 2 x\right) \int d x\right\} d x\right]_{2}^{5} \\\Rightarrow \left[x \ln 2 x-\int\left(\frac{1}{2 x} \cdot 2 x\right) d x\right]_{2}^{5}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow [x \ln 2 x-x]_{2}^{5} \\\Rightarrow 5 \ln 10-5-2 \ln 4+2 \\\Rightarrow \ln \frac{10^{5}}{16}-3=\ln \frac{5^{5} \times 2^{5}}{2^{4}}-3 \\\Rightarrow \ln \left(2 \times 5^{5}\right)-3=\ln 2+5 \ln 5-3 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{aligned}P_{1}(x) & =x \\P_{2}(x) & =\cot ^{-1} x\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} P_{1}(x) P_{2}(x) d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} x \cot ^{-1} x d x \\\Rightarrow \left[\cot ^{-1} x \int x d x-\int\left(\frac{d}{d x}\left(\cot ^{-1} x\right) \int x d x\right) d x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{2} \cot ^{-1} x}{2}-\int\left(-\frac{1}{1+x^{2}}\right) \frac{x^{2}}{2} d x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{2} \cot ^{-1} x}{2}+\int \frac{x^{2}}{2\left(1+x^{2}\right)} d x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{2} \cot ^{-1} x}{2}+\int \frac{1+x^{2}-1}{2\left(1+x^{2}\right)} d x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{2} \cot ^{-1} x}{2}+\int\left\{\frac{1}{2}-\frac{1}{2\left(1+x^{2}\right)}\right\} d x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{2} \cot ^{-1} x}{2}+\frac{x}{2}-\frac{1}{2} \int \frac{d x}{1+x^{2}}\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{2} \cot ^{-1} x}{2}+\frac{x}{2}-\frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)^{2}\left(\frac{1}{2} \cot ^{-1} \frac{\pi}{4}\right)+\frac{\pi}{8}-\frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{\pi}{4}-0-0+0 \\\Rightarrow \frac{\pi^{2}}{32} \cot ^{-1} \frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{\pi}{8}-\frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} \frac{\pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=169 \Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}=(13)^{2}[/math]
ইহা একটি বৃত্তের সমীকরণ যার কেন্দ্রের স্থানাঙ্ক [math](0, 0)[/math]
 এবং ব্যাসার্ধ [math]13[/math]
 এককএখন, [math]y^{2}=13^{2}-x^{2}[/math]
'অর্থাৎ, [math]y=\sqrt{13^{2}-x^{2}} ; x[/math]
-অক্ষের উপরের অংশে y ধনাত্মক
[Image]
[math]\therefore \mathrm{OCABO}[/math]
 ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\Rightarrow 2 \times \mathrm{OABO}[/math]
 ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \int_{0}^{13} \sqrt{(13)^{2}-x^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow 2 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sqrt{(13)^{2}-(13)^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot 13 \cos \theta d \theta\end{array}[/math]
ধরি, [math]x=13 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{dx}=13 \cos \theta \mathrm{d} \theta[/math]
যখন, [math]x=0[/math]
 তখন, [math]\theta=0[/math]
আবার, [math]x=13[/math]
 tkhn, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 169 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 2 \cos ^{2} \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow 169 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \cdot(1+\cos 2 \theta) d \theta \\\Rightarrow 169\left[\theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\left.\Rightarrow169 \cdot \frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \times \frac{\pi}{2}-0-0\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{169 \pi}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\int_{2}^{5}\ln(2x)\,dx=\int_{2}^{5}(\ln2+\ln x)\,dx=3\ln2+[x\ln x-x]_{2}^{5}= \ln2+5\ln5-3.[/math]

খ [math]\int_{0}^{\pi/4} x\cot^{-1}x\,dx[/math] এ জন্য ভাঙন প্রয়োগ করলে নিনঃ নিলে [math]u=\cot^{-1}x,\ dv=x\,dx[/math] হলে ফলস্বরূপ পাওয়া যায় [math]\left[\frac{x^{2}}{2}\cot^{-1}x\right]_{0}^{\pi/4}+\frac{1}{2}\int_{0}^{\pi/4}\frac{x^{2}}{1+x^{2}}dx[/math] এবং এটি সরল করলে এক বিকল্প রূপে পাওয়া যায় [math]\frac{\pi^{2}}{32}\cot^{-1}\!\left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+\frac{1}{2}\Big(\frac{\pi}{4}-\tan^{-1}\!\left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)\Big).[\/math]

গ ছায়াযুক্ত ক্ষেত্রফল হচ্ছে [math]\int_{0}^{\pi/4}\big(\cot^{-1}x-x\big)\,dx[/math]; অ্যান্টিডেরিভেটিভ দিয়ে মূল্যায়ন করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]\left[x\cot^{-1}x+\tfrac{1}{2}\ln(1+x^{2})-\tfrac{x^{2}}{2}\right]_{0}^{\pi/4}=(\tfrac{\pi}{4})\cot^{-1}\!\left(\tfrac{\pi}{4}\right)+\tfrac{1}{2}\ln\!\left(1+(\tfrac{\pi}{4})^{2}\right)-\tfrac{1}{2}\left(\tfrac{\pi}{4}\right)^{2}.[/math]

Question #130 (ID: 415454)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P(x)=\cos x, \frac{x^{2}}{36}+\frac{y^{2}}{25}=1 .[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \frac{d x}{1+\cos 2 x}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} x^{2} P(x) d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. উদ্দীপকের উপবৃত্ত এবং [math]x = 3[/math] রেখা দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষুদ্রতর অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{aligned}\int_{0}^{\pi / 4} \frac{1}{1+\cos 2 x} d x & =\int_{0}^{\pi / 4} \frac{1}{2 \cos ^{2} x} d x \\& \Rightarrow\frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{\pi / 4} \sec ^{2} x d x \\& \Rightarrow\frac{1}{2}[\tan x]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}=\frac{1}{2}\left[\tan \frac{\pi}{4}-0\right] \\&\Rightarrow\frac{1}{2} \cdot 1=\frac{1}{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{P}(\mathrm{x})=\cos \mathrm{x}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} x^{2} P(x) d x=\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} x^{2} \cos x d x[/math]
ধরি, [math]I=\int_{0}^{\pi / 2} x^{2} \cos x d x[/math]
এখন, [math]\int x^{2} \cos x d x \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x^{2} \int \cos x d x-\int\left\{\frac{d}{d x}\left(x^{2}\right) \int \cos x d x\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin x-\int 2 x \sin x d x \\\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin x-2\left[x \int \sin x d x-\int\left\{\frac{d}{d x}(x) \int \sin x d x\right\} d x\right] \\\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin x-2\left[x(-\cos x)-\int(-\cos x) d x\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin x-2[-x \cos x+\sin x]+c \\\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin x+2 x \cos x-2 \sin x+c \\\because I=\left[x^{2} \sin x+2 x \cos x-2 \sin x\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{\pi^{2}}{4} \sin \frac{\pi}{2}+\pi \cos \frac{\pi}{2}-2 \sin \frac{\pi}{2}\right)-(0+0-2 \sin 0) \\\Rightarrow \frac{\pi^{2}}{4}+\pi \times 0-2+0=\frac{\pi^{2}}{4}-2 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ
[Image]
[math]\frac{x^{2}}{36}+\frac{y^{2}}{25}=1\ldots \ldots\text { ... (i) }[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{x}=3 \ldots \ldots \ldots(\mathrm{ii})[/math]
(i) নং এ y = 0 বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{x^{2}}{36}=1 \\\therefore x= \pm 6\end{array}[/math]
উপবৃত্তটি x-অক্ষকে [math](6, 0)[/math]
 ও [math](– 6, 0)[/math]
 বিন্দুতে ছেদ করে(i) নং হতে, [math]\frac{y^{2}}{25}=1-\frac{x^{2}}{36}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{y^{2}}{25}=\frac{1}{36}\left(36-x^{2}\right) \\\therefore y=\frac{5}{6} \sqrt{36-x^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
(i) ও (ii) নং দ্বারা আবদ্ধ ক্ষুদ্রতর অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\Rightarrow 2 \int_{3}^{6} \frac{5}{6} \sqrt{6^{2}-x^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{5}{3}\left[\frac{x}{2} \sqrt{6^{2}-x^{2}}+\frac{6^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{6}\right]_{3}^{6} \\{\left[\because \int \sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}} d x=\frac{x}{2} \sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}+\frac{a^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{a}+c\right]}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{5}{3}\left[\left(0-\frac{3}{2} \sqrt{27}\right)+18\left(\sin ^{-1} 1-\sin ^{-1} \frac{1}{2}\right)\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{-5}{2} \times 3 \sqrt{3}+30\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow 30 \times \frac{\pi}{3}-\frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=10 \pi-\frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক কারণ [math]1+\cos2x=2\cos^2x[/math], তাই ইন্টিগ্রালটি [math]\int_{0}^{\pi/4}\frac{1}{2}\sec^2x\,dx=\frac{1}{2}\tan x\Big|_{0}^{\pi/4}=\frac{1}{2}[/math] হয়।

খ এখানে [math]P(x)=\cos x[/math], তাই ইন্টিগ্রালটি [math]\int_{0}^{\pi/2}x^2\cos x\,dx[/math] এবং অংশগত সমন্বয়ে একটি অন্তরক হচ্ছে [math]x^2\sin x+2x\cos x-2\sin x[/math]; সীমায় মূল্যায়ন করলে ফল পাওয়া যায় [math]\frac{\pi^2}{4}-2[/math]।

গ এলিপ্সটি [math]a=6,\;b=5[/math] এবং ছোট অংশটি [math]x=3[/math] থেকে [math]x=6[/math] পর্যন্ত; ক্ষেত্রফল [math]2\int_{3}^{6}5\sqrt{1-\frac{x^2}{36}}\,dx=10\int_{3}^{6}\sqrt{1-\frac{x^2}{36}}\,dx[/math] হয়। সাবসটিটিউশন [math]x=6\sin\theta[/math] দিলে এটি [math]60\int_{\pi/6}^{\pi/2}\cos^2\theta\,d\theta[/math] এবং মূল্যায়ন করলে ফল হয় [math]10\pi-\frac{15\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]।

Question #131 (ID: 415455)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=3-2 x, g(x)=3+4 x-4 x^{2}, h(x)=\sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int \sin ^{11} x \cos x d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int \frac{f(x)}{\sqrt{g(x)}} d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\int h(x) d x=\frac{x \sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}}{2}+\frac{a^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{a}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\int \sin ^{11} x \cos x d x[/math]
ধরি, [math]\sin x=z \therefore \cos x d x=d z[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\int z^{11} d z=\frac{z^{11+1}}{11+1}+c=\frac{z^{12}}{12}+c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{12} \sin ^{12} x+c \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=3-2 x[/math]
 এবং [math]g(x)=3+4 x-4 x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \int \frac{f(x)}{\sqrt{g(x)}} d x=\int \frac{3-2 x}{\sqrt{3+4 x-4 x^{2}}} d x \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{3-2 x}{\sqrt{3+4 x-4 x^{2}}} d x \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{\frac{1}{4}(4-8 x)+2}{\sqrt{3+4 x-4 x^{2}}} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int \frac{4-8 x}{\sqrt{3+4 x-4 x^{2}}} d x+\int \frac{2}{\sqrt{3+4 x-4 x^{2}}} d x \\\end{array}[/math]
[১ম পদের জন্য, [math]z=3+4 x-4 x^{2}[/math]
 হলে,][math]d z=(4-8 x) d x][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int \frac{\mathrm{dz}}{\sqrt{z}}+\int \frac{2 d x}{\sqrt{4-1+4 x-4 x^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \cdot 2 \sqrt{z}+\int \frac{2 \mathrm{dx}}{\sqrt{4-1+4 x-4 x^{2}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{z}+2 \int \frac{\mathrm{dx}}{\sqrt{2^{2}-(1-2 x)^{2}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{z}+2 \cdot\left(\sin ^{-1} \frac{1-2 x}{2}\right)-\frac{1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{3+4 x-4 x^{2}}-\sin ^{-1} \frac{1-2 x}{2}+\text { c (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]h(x)=\sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int h(x) d x=\int \sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}} d x[/math]
মনে করি, [math]x=a \sin \theta \Rightarrow d x=a \cos \theta \cdot d \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]\theta=\sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{a}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}} d x & =\int \sqrt{a^{2}-a^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot a \cos \theta d \theta \\& \Rightarrow a^{2} \int \cos ^{2} \theta d \theta=\frac{a^{2}}{2} \int(1+\cos 2 \theta) d \theta \\& \Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}}{2}\left[\theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta\right] \\& \Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}}{2} \theta+\frac{a^{2}}{2} \sin \theta \cos \theta \\& \Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}}{2} \theta+\frac{a^{2}}{2} \sin \theta \sqrt{1-\sin ^{2} \theta} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{a}+\frac{a^{2}}{2} \cdot \frac{x}{a} \sqrt{1-\frac{x^{2}}{a^{2}}} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{x \sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}}{2}+\frac{a^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{a}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int \mathrm{h}(\mathrm{x}) \mathrm{dx}=\frac{\mathrm{x} \sqrt{\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{x}^{2}}}{2}+\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{\mathrm{x}}{\mathrm{a}}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\int \sin^{11}x\cos x\,dx[/math] এলে [math]u=\sin x,\;du=\cos x\,dx[/math] ধরি, ফলে [math]\int u^{11}du=\frac{u^{12}}{12}+C=\frac{\sin^{12}x}{12}+C[/math]।

খ প্রথমে [math]g(x)=3+4x-4x^{2}=4\bigl(1-(x-\tfrac{1}{2})^{2}\bigr)[/math] লিখে, [math]u=x-\tfrac{1}{2},\;dx=du[/math] নিলে যোগফল সরল হয়: [math]\int\frac{2(1-u)}{2\sqrt{1-u^{2}}}du=\int\frac{1-u}{\sqrt{1-u^{2}}}du=\sin^{-1}u+\sqrt{1-u^{2}}+C[/math]; তাই ফল হলো [math]\sin^{-1}\!(x-\tfrac{1}{2})+\sqrt{1-(x-\tfrac{1}{2})^{2}}+C[/math]।

গ প্রমাণের জন্য [math]x=a\sin\theta,\;dx=a\cos\theta\,d\theta[/math] ধরা হলে [math]\sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}=a\cos\theta[/math] এবং ইন্টিগ্রাল হয় [math]a^{2}\int\cos^{2}\theta\,d\theta=\frac{a^{2}}{2}\bigl(\theta+\sin\theta\cos\theta\bigr)+C[/math]; ফিরে নিয়ে [math]\theta=\sin^{-1}\frac{x}{a},\;\sin\theta=\frac{x}{a},\;\cos\theta=\frac{\sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}}{a}[/math] বসালে ফল পাওয়া যায় [math]\frac{x\sqrt{a^{2}-x^{2}}}{2}+\frac{a^{2}}{2}\sin^{-1}\!\frac{x}{a}+C[/math]।

Question #132 (ID: 415452)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{x}}[/math] এবং চিত্র:


[Image]


Options:
ক. যোগজ নির্ণয় কর: [math]\int x e^{x^{2}} \cdot d x[/math]
খ. [math]\int_{0}^{3} \frac{x f(x)}{(1+x)^{2}} d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. উদ্দীপকের ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\int x e^{x^{2}} d x[/math]
ধরি, [math]\mathrm{x}^{2}=\mathrm{z} \quad \therefore 2 \mathrm{xdx}=\mathrm{dz}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{xdx}=\frac{\mathrm{dz}}{2}[/math]
এখন, [math]\int x e^{x^{2}} d x=\int e^{z} \frac{d z}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} e^{z}+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} e^{x^{2}}+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=e^{x}[/math]
মনে করি [math]I=\int_{0}^{3} \frac{x f(x)}{(1+x)^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{3} \frac{x e^{x}}{(1+x)^{2}} d x[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে ][math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{3} e^{x}\left\{\frac{1+x-1}{(1+x)^{2}}\right\} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{3} \mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{x}}\left\{\frac{1}{1+x}-\frac{1}{(1+x)^{2}}\right\} d x[/math]
এখন , ধরি, [math]f(x)=\frac{1}{1+x} \therefore f^{\prime}(x)=-\frac{1}{(1+x)^{2}}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\int e^{x}\left\{f(x)+f^{\prime}(x)\right\} d x=e^{x} f(x)+c[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int_{0}^{3} e^{x}\left\{\frac{1}{1+x}-\frac{1}{(1+x)^{2}}\right\} d x .[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left[\frac{e^{x}}{1+x}\right]_{0}^{3} \\\Rightarrow \left[\frac{e^{3}}{1+3}-\frac{e^{0}}{1+0}\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{e^{3}}{4}-1 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ
[Image]
প্রদত্ত পরাবৃত্তের সমীকরণ, [math]\mathrm{y}^{2}=4 \mathrm{x} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow y= \pm 2 \sqrt{x}[/math]
প্রথম চতুর্ভাগে পরাবৃত্তের সমীকরণ, [math]y=2 \sqrt{x}[/math]
এবং সরলরেখার সমীকরণ[math]y=x \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (iii) }[/math]
(i) নং ও (iii) নং হতে,[math]\begin{array}{l}x^{2}=4 x \\\Rightarrow x^{2}-4 x=0 \\\Rightarrow x(x-4)=0 \\\therefore x=0,4\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ছেদবিন্দুদ্বয়ের ভুজ [math]0[/math]
 ও [math]4[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\int_{0}^{4}\left(y_{1}-y_{2}\right) d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{4}(2 \sqrt{x}-x) d x=\left[2 \cdot \frac{x^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{x^{2}}{2}\right]_{0}^{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\frac{4}{3} x^{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{1}{2} x^{2}\right]_{0}^{4}=\frac{4}{3} \cdot 4^{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{1}{2} \cdot 4^{2}-0+0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{32}{3}-8=\frac{8}{3}[/math]
 বর্গ একক

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক সমাধান: পরিবর্তননামক নিলে [math]u=x^{2}[/math], ফলে [math]du=2x\,dx[/math] এবং বিস্তারিতভাবে [math]\int x e^{x^{2}}dx=\frac{1}{2}\int e^{u}du=\frac{1}{2}e^{u}+C=\frac{1}{2}e^{x^{2}}+C[/math]।

খ সমাধান: চিত্র থেকে স্পর্শক রেখার ঢাল x=0-এ [math]1[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\ln c=1[/math] এবং তাই [math]c=e[/math]. এরপর দেখা যায় [math]\frac{d}{dx}\left(\frac{e^{x}}{1+x}\right)=\frac{x e^{x}}{(1+x)^{2}}\right[/math], তাই
[math]\int_{0}^{3}\frac{x e^{x}}{(1+x)^{2}}dx=\left[\frac{e^{x}}{1+x}\right]_{0}^{3}=\frac{e^{3}}{4}-1[/math]।

গ সমাধান: উদ্দীপকের ছায়াঘেরা অংশ যদি সেই একই [math]x[/math]-ব্যবধানের নিচের ক্ষেত্রফল (অর্থাৎ [math]\int_{0}^{3}\frac{x e^{x}}{(1+x)^{2}}dx[/math]) বোঝায়, তবে তার মানও [math]\frac{e^{3}}{4}-1[/math] হবে, কারণ সেটাই উপরের নির্ণীত নির্দিষ্ট যোগজ।

Question #133 (ID: 415453)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=x \sin ^{-1} x^{2} g(x)=\frac{x^{2}}{x^{2}-4}[/math]

Options:
ক. সমাকলন কর: [math]\int 5 \cos 4 x \sin 3 x d x[/math]
খ. যোগজ নির্ণয় কর: [math]\int f(x) \mathrm{dx}[/math]
গ. [math]\int g(x) d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{aligned}\int 5 \cos 4 x \sin 3 x d x & =\frac{5}{2} \int 2 \cos 4 x \sin 3 x d x \\& \Rightarrow \frac{5}{2} \int(\sin 7 x-\sin x) d x \\& \Rightarrow \frac{5}{2}\left(-\frac{1}{7} \cos 7 x+\cos x\right)+c \\& \Rightarrow \frac{5}{14}(7 \cos x-\cos 7 x)+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x \sin ^{-1} x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int f(x) \mathrm{dx}=\int \mathrm{x} \sin ^{-1} \mathrm{x}^{2} \mathrm{dx}[/math]
ধরি,[math]\begin{aligned}I &\Rightarrow \int x \sin ^{-1} x^{2} d x \\& \Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \int \sin ^{-1} z d z\end{aligned}[/math]
ধরি, [math]x^{2}=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{xdx}=\mathrm{dz} \\\therefore \mathrm{x} \mathrm{d} \mathrm{x}=\frac{1}{2} \mathrm{dz}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[\sin ^{-1} z \int d z-\int\left\{\frac{d}{d z}\left(\sin ^{-1} z\right) \int d z\right\} d z\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[\left(\sin ^{-1} z\right) z-\int \frac{1}{\sqrt{1-z^{2}}} z d z\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[z\left(\sin ^{-1} z\right)+\frac{1}{2} \int \frac{-2 z}{\sqrt{1-z^{2}}} d z\right]^{1} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[z\left(\sin ^{-1} z\right)+\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \sqrt{1-z^{2}}\right]+c\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \int \frac{f^{\prime}(x)}{\sqrt{f(x)}} d x=2 \sqrt{f(x)}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[z \sin ^{-1} z+\sqrt{1-z^{2}}\right]+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[x^{2} \sin ^{-1}\left(x^{2}\right)+\sqrt{1-x^{4}}\right]+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]g(x)=\frac{x^{2}}{x^{2}-4}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \int g(x) d x & =\int \frac{x^{2}}{x^{2}-4} d x=\int \frac{\left(x^{2}-4\right)+4}{x^{2}-4} d x \\& \Rightarrow \int d x+4 \int \frac{d x}{x^{2}-4}=\int d x+4 \int \frac{d x}{x^{2}-2^{2}} \\& \Rightarrow x+4 \cdot \frac{1}{2 \cdot 2} \ln \left|\frac{x-2}{x+2}\right|+c \\& \Rightarrow x+\ln \left|\frac{x-2}{x+2}\right|+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক ব্যবহার করুন product-to-sum পরিচিতি: [math]\cos4x\sin3x=\tfrac{1}{2}[\sin7x-\sin x][/math], তাই [math]\int5\cos4x\sin3x\,dx=\tfrac{5}{2}\int(\sin7x-\sin x)\,dx=\tfrac{5}{2}\big(-\tfrac{1}{7}\cos7x+\cos x\big)+C[/math].

খ ইন্টিগ্রেশন বাই পার্টস নিন: [math]u=\sin^{-1}(x^2),\ dv=x\,dx[/math], তখন [math]du=\tfrac{2x}{\sqrt{1-x^4}}dx,\ v=\tfrac{x^2}{2}[/math]; হিসাব করলে [math]\int x\sin^{-1}(x^2)\,dx=\tfrac{x^2}{2}\sin^{-1}(x^2)+\tfrac{1}{2}\sqrt{1-x^4}+C[/math]।

গ বিভাজন করে লিখুন [math]\frac{x^2}{x^2-4}=1+\frac{4}{x^2-4}[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\int g(x)\,dx=\int1\,dx+4\int\frac{1}{x^2-4}\,dx=x+\ln\left|\frac{x-2}{x+2}\right|+C[/math]।

Question #134 (ID: 415451)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]h(\theta)=\tan ^{-1} \theta[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=25[/math] একটি বৃত্তের সমীকরণ।

Options:
ক. [math]\int \sqrt{1-\sin 2 x} d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int x h(x) d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. যোগজীকরণের সাহায্যে উদ্দীপকে প্রদত্ত বৃত্তের প্রথম চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\int \sqrt{1-\sin 2 x} d x \\\Rightarrow \int \sqrt{\sin ^{2} x-2 \sin x \cos x+\cos ^{2} x} \cdot d x \\\Rightarrow \int \sqrt{(\sin x-\cos x)^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \int(\sin x-\cos x) d x \\\Rightarrow --\cos x-\sin x+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]h(\theta)=\tan ^{-1} \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\int x h(x) d x=\int x \tan ^{-1} x d x \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{-1} x \int x d x-\int\left\{\frac{d}{d x}\left(\tan ^{-1} x\right) \int x d x\right\} d x \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{-1} x \cdot \frac{x^{2}}{2}-\frac{1}{2} \int \frac{1}{1+x^{2}} \cdot x^{2} d x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{2} \tan ^{-1} x-\frac{1}{2} \int \frac{x^{2}}{1+x^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{2} \tan ^{-1} x-\frac{1}{2} \int \frac{1+x^{2}-1}{1+x^{2}} d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{2} \tan ^{-1} x-\frac{1}{2} \int\left(1-\frac{1}{1+x^{2}}\right) d x \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{2} \tan ^{-1} x-\frac{1}{2}\left[x-\tan ^{-1} x\right]+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{2} \tan ^{-1} x-\frac{1}{2} x+\frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} x+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=25[/math]
 একটি বৃত্তের সমীকরণএখন, [math]y^{2}=25-x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{y}= \pm \sqrt{25-\mathrm{x}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]y=0[/math]
 হলে পাই, [math]x= \pm 5[/math]

[Image]
প্ৰথম চতুর্ভাগে [math]y=\sqrt{25-x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত বৃত্তের প্রথম চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{5} y d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{5} \sqrt{25-x^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{5} \sqrt{5^{2}-x^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x}{2} \sqrt{5^{2}-x^{2}}+\frac{5^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1}\left(\frac{x}{5}\right)\right]_{0}^{5}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 0+\frac{5^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1}(1)-0-0 \\\Rightarrow \frac{25}{2} \cdot \frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{25}{4} \pi[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক কারণ [math]1-\sin2x=(\sin x-\cos x)^2[/math], তাই [math]\sqrt{1-\sin2x}=|\sin x-\cos x|[/math]; যেখানে [math]\sin x\ge\cos x[/math] ধরে নেওয়া হলে ইন্টেগ্রালটি [math]\int(\sin x-\cos x)\,dx=-\cos x-\sin x+C[/math] হবে।  
খ [math]\int x\,h(x)\,dx=\int x\arctan x\,dx[/math] বাই-পার্টসে নিলে ([math]u=\arctan x,\ dv=x\,dx[/math]) ফল দেয় [math]\frac{x^2+1}{2}\arctan x-\frac{x}{2}+C[/math]।  
গ বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ [math]5[/math], তাই প্রথম চতুর্ভাগের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\tfrac14\pi r^2=\tfrac{25\pi}{4}[/math] (অথবা [math]\int_0^5\sqrt{25-x^2}\,dx=\tfrac{25\pi}{4}[/math])।

Question #135 (ID: 415449)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প-২: [math]h(x)=\frac{1}{x(x-1)^{2}\left(x^{2}+1\right)}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int_{0}^{1} \frac{d x}{\sqrt{1-x^{2}}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. সমাকলন কর: [math]\int h(x) d x[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ এ উল্লিখিত ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\int_{0}^{1} \frac{d x}{\sqrt{1-x^{2}}} \\\Rightarrow \left[\sin ^{-1} x\right]_{0}^{1} \\\Rightarrow \sin ^{-1}(1)-\sin ^{-1}(0) \\\Rightarrow \frac{\pi}{2}-0=\frac{\pi}{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]h(x)=\frac{1}{x(x-1)^{2}\left(x^{2}+1\right)}[/math]
মনে করি, [math]\frac{1}{x(x-1)^{2}\left(x^{2}+1\right)} \equiv \frac{A}{x}+\frac{B}{x-1}+\frac{C}{(x-1)^{2}}+\frac{D x+E}{x^{2}+1} \ldots \text { ... (i) }[/math]
উভয়পক্ষকে [math]{x}(x-1)^{2}\left(x^{2}+1\right)[/math]
 দ্বারা গুণ করে পাই,[math]1 \equiv A(x-1)^{2}\left(x^{2}+1\right)+B x(x-1)\left(x^{2}+1\right)+C x\left(x^{2}+1\right)+(D x+E) x(x-1)^{2}\ldots \text { ... (ii) }[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1 \equiv \mathrm{A}\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}-2 \mathrm{x}+1\right)\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+1\right)+\mathrm{Bx}(\mathrm{x}-1)\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+1\right)+C x\left(x^{2}+1\right)+(D x+E) x\left(x^{2}-2 x+1\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1 \equiv A\left(x^{4}-2 x^{3}+2 x^{2}-2 x+1\right)+B\left(x^{4}-x^{3}+x^{2}-x\right)+C\left(x^{3}+x\right)+D\left(x^{4}-2 x^{3}+x^{2}\right)E\left(x^{3}-2 x^{2}+x\right) \ldots\text { ... (iii) }[/math]
 [math]x=0[/math]
 হলে (ii) নং হতে পাই, [math]A = 1[/math]
 [math]x = 1[/math]
 হলে (ii) নং হতে পাই, [math]1=C \cdot 1 \cdot\left(1^{2}+1\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{C}=1 \therefore C=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
(iii) নং এর উভয়পক্ষে [math]x^{4}, x^{3}, x^{2}[/math]
 ও [math]x[/math]
 এর সহগ সমীকৃত করে পাই,[math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{D}=0 \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (iv) }[/math]
 [math]-2 A-B+C-2 D+E=0 \ldots\text { ... (v) }[/math]
 [math]-2 A-B+C+E=0 \ldots \ldots \text { (vi) }[/math]
 [math]A[/math]
 এবং [math]C[/math]
 এর মান [math](iv), (v)[/math]
 ও [math](vi)[/math]
 নং সমীকরণে বসিয়ে পাই,[math]1+B+D=0 \Rightarrow B=-D-1 \ldots \ldots \text { (vii) }[/math]
এবং [math]-2.1-B+\frac{1}{2}-2 D+E=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{D}+1-2 \mathrm{D}+\mathrm{E}=\frac{3}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{E}=\frac{1}{2}+\mathrm{D} \ldots \ldots \text { (viii) }\end{array}[/math]
এবং [math]-2.1-B+\frac{1}{2}+E=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{D}+1+\frac{\mathrm{1}}{2}+\mathrm{D}-2+\frac{1}{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{D}=0 \therefore \mathrm{D}=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]D[/math]
 এর মান (vii) ও (viii) নং এ বসিয়ে পাই,[math]B=-1[/math]
 এবং [math]E=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
(i) নং এ [math]A, B, C, D[/math]
 ও [math]E[/math]
 এর মান বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}h(x)=\frac{1}{x(x-1)^{2}\left(x^{2}+1\right)} \equiv \frac{1}{x}+\frac{-1}{x-1}+\frac{1}{2(x-1)^{2}}+\frac{1}{2\left(x^{2}+1\right)} \\\begin{aligned}\therefore & \int h(x) d x \\& \Rightarrow \int\left[\frac{1}{x}-\frac{1}{x-1}+\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{1}{(x-1)^{2}}+\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{1}{1+x^{2}}\right] d x \\& \Rightarrow \ln |x|-\ln (|x-1|)-\frac{1}{2(x-1)}+\frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} x+c \\& \Rightarrow \ln \left|\frac{x}{x-1}\right|-\frac{1}{2(x-1)}+\frac{1}{2} \tan ^{-1} x+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গপ্রদত্ত পরাবৃত্তের সমীকরণ, [math]y^{2}=2 x \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
এবং সরলরেখার সমীকরণ, [math]y=x \ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }[/math]
(i) ও (ii) নং হতে পাই, [math]x^{2}=2 x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x^{2}-2 x=0\\\Rightarrow x(x-2)=0\\\therefore \mathrm{x}=0,2 \text{.}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ছেদবিন্দুদ্বয়ের ভুজ [math]0[/math]
 ও [math]2[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\int_{0}^{2}\left(y_{1}-y_{2}\right) d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{2}(\sqrt{2} \cdot \sqrt{x}-x) d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\sqrt{2} \frac{x^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{x^{2}}{2}\right]_{0}^{2}=\left[\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{3} x^{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{1}{2} x^{2}\right]_{2}^{0}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\{\left(\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{3} \cdot 2^{\frac{3}{2}}-\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2^{2}\right) = 0\right\} \frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{3} \cdot 2 \sqrt{2}-2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{8}{3}-2=\frac{8-6}{3}=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\displaystyle \int_{0}^{1}\frac{dx}{\sqrt{1-x^{2}}}=\arcsin x\Big|_{0}^{1}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]—কারণ [math]\frac{d}{dx}(\arcsin x)=\frac{1}{\sqrt{1-x^{2}}}[/math]।

খ অংশে পার্শ্বভগ্নাংশ করলে [math]h(x)=\frac{1}{x(x-1)^{2}(x^{2}+1)}=\frac{1}{x}-\frac{1}{x-1}+\frac{1}{2(x-1)^{2}}+\frac{1}{2}\frac{1}{x^{2}+1}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, তাই সমাকলন হলো [math]\int h(x)\,dx=\ln|x|-\ln|x-1|-\frac{1}{2(x-1)}+\frac{1}{2}\arctan x+C[/math]।

গ ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফলটি ক অংশের সমাকলনেই দেওয়া, তাই ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]।

Question #136 (ID: 415450)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\frac{1}{1+\sin x-\cos x}, g(x)=\frac{2+x}{1+x^{2}}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sin x d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. x এর সাপেক্ষে [math]f(x)[/math] এর সমাকলন কর।
গ. [math]0[/math] থেকে [math]1[/math] সীমার মধ্যে [math]\int g(x) d x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sin x d x=[-\cos x]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(-\cos \frac{\pi}{2}\right)-(-\cos 0)=0-(-1)=1 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওইয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\frac{1}{1+\sin x-\cos x}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int f(x) d x=\int \frac{1}{1+\sin \mathrm{x}-\cos \mathrm{x}} \mathrm{dx}=\int \frac{1}{1+\sin 2 \cdot \frac{\mathrm{x}}{2}-\cos 2 \cdot \frac{\mathrm{x}}{2}} d \mathrm{x}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int \frac{1}{1+\frac{2 \tan \frac{x}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}-\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}} d x[/math]
 [math]\int \dfrac{1}{\dfrac{1+\tan^{2}\dfrac{x}{2}+2\tan\dfrac{x}{2}-1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}}dx[/math]
ধরি, [math]\tan \frac{x}{2}=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\frac{1}{2} \sec ^{2} \frac{x}{2} d x=d z \\\therefore \sec ^{2} \frac{x}{2} d x=2 d z\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int \frac{1+\tan^2 \frac{ x}{2}}{2 \tan^2 \frac{x}{2}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int \frac{\sec ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{2 \tan^2 \frac{x}{2}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 d z}{2 z^{2}+2 z} \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{2 d z}{2 z^{2}+2 z} \\\Rightarrow \int \frac{1}{z^{2}+z} d z\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\int \frac{1}{z(z+1)} d z=\int\left\{\frac{1}{z(0+1)}+\frac{1}{(z+1)(-1)}\right\} d z[/math]
 [math]=\int\left(\frac{1}{z}-\frac{1}{z+1}\right) d z=\ln |z| - \ln (|z+1|)+\mathrm{c}[/math]
 [math]=\ln \left|\frac{{z}}{z+1}\right|+c=\ln \left|\frac{\tan \frac{x}{2}}{\tan \frac{x}{2}+1}\right|+c \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{g}(\mathrm{x})=\frac{2+\mathrm{x}}{1+\mathrm{x}^{2}} \\\therefore \int_{0}^{1} \mathrm{~g}(\mathrm{x}) \mathrm{dx}=\int_{0}^{1} \frac{2+\mathrm{x}}{1+\mathrm{x}^{2}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{1} \frac{2}{1+\mathrm{x}^{2}} \mathrm{dx}+\int_{0}^{1} \frac{\mathrm{x}}{1+\mathrm{x}^{2}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow 2\left[\tan ^{-1} \mathrm{x}\right]_{0}^{1}+\frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{1} \frac{2 \mathrm{x}}{1+\mathrm{x}^{2}} \mathrm{dx} \\\Rightarrow 2\left[\tan ^{-1} \mathrm{x}\right]_{0}^{1}+\frac{1}{2}\left[\ln \left(1+\mathrm{x}^{2}\right)\right]_{0}^{1} \\\Rightarrow 2\left(\tan ^{-1} 1-\tan ^{-1} 0\right)+\frac{1}{2}(\ln 2-\ln 1) \\\Rightarrow 2\left(\frac{\pi}{4}-0\right)+\frac{1}{2} \ln 2 \\\Rightarrow \frac{\pi}{2}+\ln 2^{\frac{1}{2}}=\frac{\pi}{2}+\ln \sqrt{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\sin x\,dx=[- \cos x]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}=(-\cos\frac{\pi}{2})-(-\cos 0)=0-(-1)=1[/math]।

খ সমাকলন করতে [math]t=\tan\frac{x}{2}[/math] (Weierstrass) ধরলে [math]\sin x=\frac{2t}{1+t^{2}},\ \cos x=\frac{1-t^{2}}{1+t^{2}},\ dx=\frac{2\,dt}{1+t^{2}}[/math] হয় এবং ইন্টেগ্র্যান্ডটি সরল হয়ে যায় [math]\int\frac{dt}{t(t+1)}=\ln\left|\frac{t}{t+1}\right|+C[/math], ফলে [math]\displaystyle \int f(x)\,dx=\ln\left|\frac{\tan(x/2)}{1+\tan(x/2)}\right|+C[/math]।

গ [math]\int_{0}^{1}\frac{2+x}{1+x^{2}}dx=\int_{0}^{1}\frac{2}{1+x^{2}}dx+\int_{0}^{1}\frac{x}{1+x^{2}}dx= [2\arctan x+\tfrac{1}{2}\ln(1+x^{2})]_{0}^{1}=\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{1}{2}\ln 2[/math]।

Question #137 (ID: 415446)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প: [math]f(y)=y, g(x, y)=x^{2}+y^{2}-225[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int \ln 7 x d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\int_{0}^{8} f\left(x^{2}\right) \sqrt{64-f\left(x^{2}\right)} d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]g(x, y)=0[/math] দ্বারা x অক্ষের উপরিভাগে আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\int \ln 7 x d x \\\Rightarrow \ln 7 x \int d x-\int\left[\frac{d}{d x}(\ln 7 x) \int d x\right] d x \\\Rightarrow x \ln 7 x-\int \frac{1}{7 x} \cdot x d x \\\Rightarrow x \ln 7 x-\int d x \\\Rightarrow x \ln 7 x-x+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(y)=y[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int_{0}^{8} f\left(x^{2}\right) \sqrt{64-f\left(x^{2}\right)} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{8} x^{2} \sqrt{64-x^{2}} d x[/math]
ধরি, [math]x=8 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{dx}=8 \cos \theta \mathrm{dx}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline \mathrm{x} & 8 & 0 \\\hline \theta & \frac{\pi}{2} & 0 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}(8 \sin \theta)^{2} \sqrt{64-(8 \sin \theta)^{2}} 8 \cos \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 64 \sin ^{2} \theta \sqrt{64-64 \sin ^{2} \theta} \cdot 8 \cos \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 64 \sin ^{2} \theta \sqrt{64\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)} \cdot 8 \cos \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 64 \sin ^{2} \theta \cdot \sqrt{64 \cos ^{2} \theta} \cdot \cos \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 64 \sin ^{2} \theta \cdot 64 \cos ^{2} \theta d \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1024 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 4 \sin ^{2} \theta \cos ^{2} \theta d \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1024 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}(2 \sin \theta \cos \theta)^{2} d \theta \\\Rightarrow 1024 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sin ^{2} 2 \theta d \theta=512 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} 2 \sin ^{2} 2 \theta d \theta \\\Rightarrow 512 \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}(1-\cos 4 \theta) d \theta=512\left[\theta-\frac{\sin 4 \theta}{4}\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \\\Rightarrow 512\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\sin 4 \frac{\pi}{2}}{4}\right)-0=512\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-0\right) \\\Rightarrow 512 \times \frac{\pi}{2}=256 \pi \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]g(x, y)=x^{2}+y^{2}-225[/math]
 [math]g(x, y)=0[/math]
 হলে,[math]\begin{array}{l}x^{2}+y^{2}-225=0 \\\Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}=225\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{2}+y^{2}=(15)^{2}....[/math]
 (i)যা একটি বৃত্তের সমীকরণ ।
[Image]
(i) নং বৃত্তের কেন্দ্রের স্থানাঙ্ক [math](0, 0)[/math]
 এবং ব্যাসার্ধ [math]15[/math]
 একক ।(i) নং হতে পাই, [math]y^{2}=15^{2}-x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{y}= \pm \sqrt{15^{2}-\mathrm{x}^{2}}[/math]
অক্ষের উপরিভাগে y ধনাত্মক ।অর্থাৎ, [math]y=\sqrt{15^{2}-x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{x}[/math]
 অক্ষের উপরিভাগে আবদ্ধ ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\Rightarrow 2 \times \mathrm{OABO}[/math]
 ক্ষেত্রের ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\Rightarrow 2 \int_{0}^{15} \sqrt{15^{2}-\mathrm{x}^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2\left[\frac{x \sqrt{15^{2}-x^{2}}}{2}+\frac{15^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{x}{15}\right]_{0}^{15} \\\Rightarrow 2\left[\left(\frac{15 \sqrt{15^{2}-15^{2}}}{2}+\frac{15^{2}}{2} \sin ^{-1} \frac{15}{15}\right)-0\right] \\\Rightarrow 2\left(0+\frac{225}{2} \sin ^{-1} 1\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 225 \cdot \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{225 \pi}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\int \ln(7x)\,dx[/math] = ব্যবহার করলে ইন্টিগ্রেশন বাই পার্টস বা [math]\ln(7x)=\ln7+\ln x[/math] ব্যবহারে পাওয়া যায় [math]x\ln(7x)-x+C[/math]। (কারণ [math]u=\ln(7x),\ dv=dx\Rightarrow v=x,\ du=dx/x[/math])

খ এখানে [math]f(y)=y[/math] হওয়ায় [math]f(x^2)=x^2[/math], ফলে ইন্টেগ্রাল হচ্ছে [math]\int_{0}^{8}x^2\sqrt{64-x^2}\,dx[/math]। ট্রিগোনোমেট্রিক substitution [math]x=8\sin\theta[/math] ( bounds [math]0\to0[/math], [math]8\to\pi/2[/math]) দিলে ইন্টিগ্র্যান্ড সিম্প্লিফাই হয়ে [math]512(1-\cos4\theta)[/math] ধাঁচে হয় এবং সম্পূর্ণ করে ফল পাওয়া যায় [math]256\pi[/math]।

গ [math]g(x,y)=0[/math] দ্বারা রচিত হল বৃত্ত [math]x^2+y^2=225[/math] যার ব্যাসার্ধ [math]15[/math]; x অক্ষের উপরিভাগে এর ক্ষেত্রফল বৃত্তের অর্ধেক, অর্থাৎ [math]\frac{1}{2}\pi(15)^2=\frac{225\pi}{2}[/math]।

Question #138 (ID: 415447)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\sin x-\cos x[/math] [math]g(x)=x^{4}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int\{f(\mathrm{x})\}^{2} \mathrm{dx}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\int \frac{1-f(x)}{1+f(x)} d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. প্রমাণ কর, [math]\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} g(\cos \theta) d \theta=\frac{3 \pi}{32}+\frac{1}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\sin x-\cos x[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\int\{f(x)\}^{2} d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int(\sin x-\cos x)^{2} d x \\\Rightarrow \int\left(\sin ^{2} x+\cos ^{2} x-2 \sin x \cos x\right) d x \\\Rightarrow \int(1-\sin 2 x) d x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x-\left(\frac{-\cos 2 x}{2}\right)+c \\\left.\Rightarrow x+\frac{\cos 2 x}{2}+c \text { (Ans. }\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\sin x-\cos x[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int \frac{1-f(x)}{1+f(x)} d x=\int \frac{1-\sin x+\cos x}{1+\sin x-\cos x} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int \frac{-(1+\sin x-\cos x)+2}{(1+\sin x-\cos x)} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -\int d x+2 \int \frac{1}{1+\sin x-\cos x} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -x+2 \int \frac{1}{1+\frac{2 \tan \frac{x}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}-\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -x+2 \int \frac{\left(1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}\right) d x}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}-1+\tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -x+2 \int \frac{\sec ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}{2 \tan ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -x+2 \int \frac{d z}{z^{2}+z}[/math]
 [ ধরি [math]\left.z=\tan \frac{x}{2} \therefore d z=\frac{1}{2} \sec ^{2} \frac{x}{2} d x\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -x+2 \int \frac{d z}{z(z+1)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -x+2 \int\left(\frac{1}{z}-\frac{1}{z+1}\right) d z \\\Rightarrow -x+2 \ln z-2 \ln (z+1)+c \\\Rightarrow -x+2 \ln \frac{z}{z+1}+c \\\Rightarrow -x+2 \ln \frac{\tan \frac{x}{2}}{1+\tan \frac{x}{2}}+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]g(x)=x^{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore g(\cos \theta)=(\cos \theta)^{4}=\cos ^{4} \theta[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} g(\cos \theta) d \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \cos ^{4} \theta \cdot d \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\left(2 \cos ^{2} \theta\right)^{2} d \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}(1+\cos 2 \theta)^{2} d \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\left(1+2 \cos 2 \theta+\cos ^{2} 2 \theta\right) d \theta \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\left(1+2 \cos 2 \theta+\frac{1}{2} \cdot \cos ^{2} 2 \theta\right) d \theta \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\left\{1+2 \cos 2 \theta+\frac{1}{2}(1+\cos 4 \theta)\right\} d \theta \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\left(1+\frac{1}{2}+2 \cos 2 \theta+\frac{1}{2} \cos 4 \theta\right) d \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\left(\frac{3}{2}+2 \cos 2 \theta+\frac{1}{2} \cos 4 \theta\right) d \theta \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4}\left[\frac{3}{2} \theta+\sin 2 \theta+\frac{1}{8} \sin 4 \theta\right]_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4}\left[\frac{3}{2} \cdot \frac{\theta}{4}+\sin \left(2 \cdot \frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{1}{8}\right) \cdot \sin \left(4 \cdot \frac{\pi}{4}\right)-0-0-0\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{4}\left[\frac{3 \pi}{8}+1+0\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{3 \pi}{32}+\frac{1}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}} g(\cos \theta) d \theta=\frac{3 \pi}{32}+\frac{1}{4}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ক [math](\sin x-\cos x)^2=\sin^2x+\cos^2x-2\sin x\cos x=1-\sin2x[/math], তাই [math]\int(\sin x-\cos x)^2dx=\int(1-\sin2x)dx=x+\tfrac{1}{2}\cos2x+C[/math]।

খ শুরুতে লিখি [math]\frac{1-f}{1+f}=-1+\frac{2}{1+f}[/math], সুতরাং [math]\int\frac{1-f}{1+f}dx=-x+2\int\frac{dx}{1+\sin x-\cos x}+C[/math]. আধা-কোণিক পরিবর্তনী [math]t=\tan\frac{x}{2}[/math] দিলে [math]1+\sin x-\cos x=\frac{2t(t+1)}{1+t^2}[/math] এবং [math]dx=\frac{2\,dt}{1+t^2}[/math], ফলে অভ্যন্তরীণ অংশ [math]\int\frac{dx}{1+\sin x-\cos x}=\int\frac{dt}{t(t+1)}=\ln\left|\frac{t}{t+1}\right|+C[/math]. অতএব ফল [math]-x+2\ln\left|\frac{\tan(x/2)}{1+\tan(x/2)}\right|+C[/math]।

গ এখানে [math]g(\cos\theta)=\cos^4\theta[/math] এবং [math]\cos^4\theta=\tfrac{3}{8}+\tfrac{1}{2}\cos2\theta+\tfrac{1}{8}\cos4\theta[/math], তাই সীমার ভিতরে সমাকলন দিলে [math]\int_{0}^{\pi/4}\cos^4\theta\,d\theta=\left[\tfrac{3}{8}\theta+\tfrac{1}{4}\sin2\theta+\tfrac{1}{32}\sin4\theta\right]_0^{\pi/4}=\tfrac{3\pi}{32}+\tfrac{1}{4}[/math]।

Question #139 (ID: 415448)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=x^{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\int \frac{5 e^{2 x}}{1+e^{4 x}} d x[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\int\left[\frac{1+\{f(x)\}^{2}}{1+f(\mathrm{x})}+\frac{1}{f(\mathrm{x})+\sqrt{f(\mathrm{x})}+1}\right] \mathrm{dx}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\int_{1}^{2}\left[\sqrt{f(x)} \mathrm{e}^{f(x)}+\frac{\{f(x)-1\}^{2}}{f(\mathrm{x})}\right] \mathrm{dx}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, [math]I=\int \frac{5 e^{2 x}}{1+e^{4 x}}[/math]
 [math]=\int \frac{5 \mathrm{e}^{2 \mathrm{x}}}{1+\left(\mathrm{e}^{2 x}\right)^{2}} d x[/math]
ধরি, [math]e^{2 x}=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{e}^{2 \mathrm{x}} \mathrm{dx}=\mathrm{dz} \\\therefore \mathrm{e}^{2 \mathrm{x}} \mathrm{dx}=\frac{\mathrm{dz}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]I=\int \frac{\frac{5}{2} d z}{1+z^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{5}{2} \int \frac{1}{1+z^{2}} d z \\\Rightarrow \frac{5}{2} \tan ^{-1} z+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{5}{2} \tan ^{-1}\left(\mathrm{e}^{2 x}\right)+\mathrm{c} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x^{2}[/math]
এখন, [math]\int\left[\frac{1+\{f(x)\}^{2}}{1+f(x)}+\frac{1}{f(x)+\sqrt{f(x)}+1}\right] d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int\left(\frac{1+x^{4}}{1+x^{2}}+\frac{1}{x^{2}+x+1}\right) d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int \frac{\left(1+x^{2}\right)^{2}-2 x^{2}}{1+x^{2}} d x+\int \frac{1}{x^{2}+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{4}+\frac{3}{4}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \int\left(1+x^{2}-2 \cdot \frac{x^{2}}{1+x^{2}}\right) d x+\int \frac{1}{\left(x+\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}+\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{2}} d x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x+\frac{x^{3}}{3}-2 \int \frac{1+x^{2}-1}{1+x^{2}} d x+\frac{1}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}} \tan ^{-1} \frac{x+\frac{1}{2}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x+\frac{x^{3}}{3}-2\left[\int d x-\int \frac{d x}{1+x^{2}}\right]+\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}} \tan ^{-1}\left\{\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}\left(x+\frac{1}{2}\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x+\frac{x^{3}}{3}-2 x+2 \tan ^{-1} x+\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}} \tan ^{-1} \frac{2 x+1}{\sqrt{3}}+c \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{3}}{3}+2 \tan ^{-1} x+\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}} \tan ^{-1} \frac{2 x+1}{\sqrt{3}}-x+c \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x^{2}[/math]
এখন [math]\int_{1}^{2}\left[\sqrt{f(x)} \cdot e^{f(x)}+\frac{\{f(x)-1\}^{2}}{f(x)}\right] d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \int_{1}^{2}\left[x \cdot e^{x^{2}}+\frac{\left(x^{2}-1\right)^{2}}{x^{2}}\right] d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{1}^{2}\left[x \cdot e^{x^{2}}+\left(\frac{x^{4}-2 x^{2}+1}{x^{2}}\right)\right] d x \\\Rightarrow \int_{1}^{2} x e^{x^{2}} d x+\int_{1}^{2}\left(x^{2}-2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right) d x\end{array}[/math]
এখন ,ধরি, [math]x^{2}=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{x} \mathrm{dx}=\mathrm{dz} \\\therefore \mathrm{xdx}=\frac{1}{2} \mathrm{dz}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|}\hline x & 2 & 1 \\\hline z & 4 & 1 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \int_{1}^{2} \mathrm{xe}^{\mathrm{x}^{2}} \mathrm{dx}=\frac{1}{2} \int_{1}^{4} \mathrm{e}^{z} \mathrm{dz}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{z}}\right]_{1}^{4}=\frac{1}{2}\left(\mathrm{e}^{4}-\mathrm{e}\right)[/math]
আবার, [math]\int_{1}^{2}\left(x^{2}-2+x^{-2}\right) d x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left[\frac{x^{3}}{3}-2 x+\frac{x^{-2+1}}{-2+1}\right]_{1}^{2}=\left[\frac{x^{3}}{3}-2 x-\frac{1}{x}\right]_{1}^{2} \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{2^{3}}{3}-2.2-\frac{1}{2}\right)-\left(\frac{1}{3}-2-1\right) \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{8}{3}-4-\frac{1}{2}\right)-\left(\frac{1}{3}-3\right) \\\Rightarrow -\frac{11}{6}+\frac{8}{3}=\frac{5}{6} \\\therefore \int_{1}^{2} x e^{x^{2}} \mathrm{dx}+\int_{1}^{2}\left(x^{2}-2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right) \mathrm{dx}=\frac{1}{2}\left(e^{4}-e\right)+\frac{5}{6} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ক প্রথমে [math]u=e^{2x}[/math] নিলে [math]du=2e^{2x}dx[/math] হয়, তাই ইন্টিগ্রলটি হয় [math]\frac{5}{2}\int\frac{du}{1+u^{2}}=\frac{5}{2}\arctan u +C=\frac{5}{2}\arctan(e^{2x})+C[/math]।

খ এখানে [math]f(x)=x^{2}[/math]; প্রথম ভগ্নাংশটি সরলীকরণ করে [math]\frac{1+x^{4}}{1+x^{2}}=x^{2}-1+\frac{2}{1+x^{2}}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, এবং দ্বিতীয়টি (ধরি [math]x\ge0[/math] হলে [math]\sqrt{f(x)}=x[/math]) হবে [math]\frac{1}{x^{2}+x+1}=\frac{1}{(x+\tfrac{1}{2})^{2}+\tfrac{3}{4}}[/math]। ফলে সমাধানটি হচ্ছে  
[math]\int\cdots dx=\frac{x^{3}}{3}-x+2\arctan x+\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan\frac{2x+1}{\sqrt{3}}+C[/math] (সাধারণ ক্ষেত্রে [math]x[/math]-এর স্থানে [math]|x|[/math] নিতে হবে)।

গ [math]x\in[1,2][/math]-এ [math]\sqrt{f(x)}=x[/math], তাই অন্তর্গত সমীকরণটি হচ্ছে [math]x e^{x^{2}}+\frac{(x^{2}-1)^{2}}{x^{2}}=x e^{x^{2}}+x^{2}-2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]; প্রথম অংশের অনির্দিষ্ট ইন্টিগ্রাল [math]\tfrac{1}{2}e^{x^{2}}[/math] এবং দ্বিতীয় অংশের ইন্টিগ্রাল থেকে সীমাবদ্ধ মান বের করলে মোট থাকে  
[math]\frac{1}{2}(e^{4}-e)+\frac{5}{6}[/math]।
